set_property(TARGET cmake_extadv_test.elf APPEND_STRING
														PROPERTY
														COMPILE_FLAGS
														"-mcpu=cortex-m4 -mthumb-interwork -mthumb -Wall -Werror -fno-exceptions -ffunction-sections -fdata-sections -Og -ggdb")

							PROPERTIES
							ARCHIVE_OUTPUT_DIRECTORY /Users/marcus/projects/lumigrow/mynewt/advext_test/bin/targets/wall_advaux/app/apps/extadv_test
